<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of minor planets: 4001–5000</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">  (Redirected from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/index.php?title=4976_Choukyongchol&amp;redirect=no" title="4976 Choukyongchol">4976 Choukyongchol</a>)</span></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><p>This is a partial list of <a href="/wiki/Minor_planet_designation" title="Minor planet designation">numbered</a> <a href="/wiki/Minor_planet" title="Minor planet">minor planets</a>, running from 4001 through 5000, inclusive. See <a href="/wiki/List_of_minor_planets#Main_index" title="List of minor planets">List of minor planets § Main index</a> for a list of all such partial lists. Also see the corresponding <a href="/wiki/Meanings_of_minor_planet_names:_4001%E2%80%935000" title="Meanings of minor planet names: 4001–5000">Meanings of minor planet names: 4001–5000</a> for details on any named body in this range.<br/></p>

<tr>
<td><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:1px #aaa solid; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#FFC2E0; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;"> </span> <a href="/wiki/Near-Earth_object" title="Near-Earth object">Near-Earth obj.</a>  </span></td>
<td><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:1px #aaa solid; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#fefefe; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;"> </span> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Inner_Main-belt_Asteroid" title="Inner Main-belt Asteroid">MBA (inner)</a></span></td>
<td><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:1px #aaa solid; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#d6d6d6; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;"> </span> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Outer_Main-belt_Asteroid" title="Outer Main-belt Asteroid">MBA (outer)</a></span></td>
<td><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:1px #aaa solid; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#C7FF8F; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;"> </span> <a href="/wiki/Centaur_(minor_planet)" title="Centaur (minor planet)">Centaur</a></span></td>

<td><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:1px #aaa solid; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#C2E0FF; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;"> </span> <a href="/wiki/Trans-Neptunian_object" title="Trans-Neptunian object">Trans-Neptunian obj.</a></span></td>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="4101.E2.80.934200">4101–4200</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_minor_planets:_4001%E2%80%935000&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 4101–4200">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><span id="101"></span></p>
<div style="float:right;"><a href="#top">back to top</a> <a href="#top" title="#top"><img alt="WWC arrow up.png" data-file-height="11" data-file-width="11" height="11" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/ce/WWC_arrow_up.png" width="11"/></a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="4601.E2.80.934700">4601–4700</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_minor_planets:_4001%E2%80%935000&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 4601–4700">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
